<td class="mbox-image"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Commons-logo.svg"><img alt="" class="noviewer" data-file-height="1376" data-file-width="1024" height="40" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/30px-Commons-logo.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/45px-Commons-logo.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/4/4a/Commons-logo.svg/59px-Commons-logo.svg.png 2x" width="30"/></a></td>
<td class="mbox-text plainlist">Wikimedia Commons has media related to <i><b><a class="extiw" href="https://commons.wikimedia.org/wiki/Category:1998" title="commons:Category:1998">1998</a></b></i>.</td>
</tr>
</table>
<p><b>1998 (<a href="/wiki/Roman_numerals" title="Roman numerals">MCMXCVIII</a>)</b> was a <a href="/wiki/Common_year" title="Common year">common year</a> <a href="/wiki/Common_year_starting_on_Thursday" title="Common year starting on Thursday">starting on Thursday</a> (<a href="/wiki/Dominical_letter" title="Dominical letter">dominical letter</a> D) of the <a href="/wiki/Gregorian_calendar" title="Gregorian calendar">Gregorian calendar</a>, the 1998th year of the <a href="/wiki/Common_Era" title="Common Era">Common Era</a> (CE) and <i><a href="/wiki/Anno_Domini" title="Anno Domini">Anno Domini</a></i> (AD) designations, the 998th year of the <a href="/wiki/2nd_millennium" title="2nd millennium">2nd millennium</a>, the 98th year of the <a href="/wiki/20th_century" title="20th century">20th century</a>, and the 9th year of the <a href="/wiki/1990s" title="1990s">1990s</a> decade.</p>
<p>1998 was designated as the <i>International Year of the Ocean</i>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Events">Events</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Events">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="January">January</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: January">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_2" title="January 2">January 2</a> – Russia begins to circulate new <a href="/wiki/Russian_ruble" title="Russian ruble">rubles</a> to stem inflation and promote confidence.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_4" title="January 4">January 4</a> – <a href="/wiki/Wilaya_of_Relizane_massacres_of_4_January_1998" title="Wilaya of Relizane massacres of 4 January 1998">Wilaya of Relizane massacres of 4 January 1998</a> in <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a>: Over 170 are killed in 3 remote villages.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_6" title="January 6">January 6</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Lunar_Prospector" title="Lunar Prospector">Lunar Prospector</a> spacecraft is launched into orbit around the <a href="/wiki/Moon" title="Moon">Moon</a>, and later finds evidence for frozen water, in soil in permanently shadowed craters near the Moon's poles.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_8" title="January 8">January 8</a> – <a href="/wiki/Ramzi_Yousef" title="Ramzi Yousef">Ramzi Yousef</a> is sentenced to life in prison for planning the first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/World_Trade_Center_bombing" title="World Trade Center bombing">World Trade Center bombing</a> in <a href="/wiki/1993" title="1993">1993</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_11" title="January 11">January 11</a> – Over 100 people are killed in the <a href="/wiki/Sidi-Hamed_massacre" title="Sidi-Hamed massacre">Sidi-Hamed massacre</a> in <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_12" title="January 12">January 12</a> – Nineteen European nations agree to forbid <a href="/wiki/Human_cloning" title="Human cloning">human cloning</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_14" title="January 14">January 14</a> – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ralph_Guarino" title="Ralph Guarino">Ralph Guarino</a> is arrested for attempting to <a href="/wiki/1998_Bank_of_America_robbery" title="1998 Bank of America robbery">rob</a> a <a href="/wiki/Bank_of_America" title="Bank of America">Bank of America</a> bank in the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/World_Trade_Center_(1973-2001)" title="World Trade Center (1973-2001)">World Trade Center</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_17" title="January 17">January 17</a> – The <i><a href="/wiki/Drudge_Report" title="Drudge Report">Drudge Report</a></i> breaks the story about U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a>'s alleged affair with <a href="/wiki/Monica_Lewinsky" title="Monica Lewinsky">Monica Lewinsky</a>, which would lead to the <a href="/wiki/United_States_House_of_Representatives" title="United States House of Representatives">House of Representatives</a>' impeachment of him.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_20" title="January 20">January 20</a> – <a href="/wiki/Nepal" title="Nepal">Nepalese</a> police intercept a shipment of 272 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Human_skull" title="Human skull">human skulls</a> in <a href="/wiki/Kathmandu" title="Kathmandu">Kathmandu</a><sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (June 2011)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_22" title="January 22">January 22</a> – Suspected "<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Unabomber" title="Unabomber">Unabomber</a>" <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Theodore_Kaczynski" title="Theodore Kaczynski">Theodore Kaczynski</a> pleads guilty, and accepts a sentence of life without the possibility of parole.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/January_28" title="January 28">January 28</a>
<ul>
<li>Gunmen hold at least 400 children and teachers hostage for several hours, at an elementary school in <a href="/wiki/Manila" title="Manila">Manila</a>, Philippines.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Stade_de_France" title="Stade de France">Stade de France</a>, as known well for sports venues of France, officially opened in Saint-Denis, suburb of <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a>, before <a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1998 FIFA World Cup">1998 FIFA World Cup</a>.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">[<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (November 2016)">citation needed</span></a></i>]</sup></li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>

<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Rouble.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="317" data-file-width="610" height="114" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Rouble.jpg/220px-Rouble.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Rouble.jpg/330px-Rouble.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1a/Rouble.jpg/440px-Rouble.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="February">February</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: February">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_1" title="February 1">February 1</a> – The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Senate" title="United States Senate">United States Senate</a> passes Resolution 71, urging U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a> to "take all necessary and appropriate actions to respond to the threat posed by <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>'s refusal to end its weapons of mass destruction programs".</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_3" title="February 3">February 3</a> – <a href="/wiki/Cavalese_cable_car_disaster_(1998)" title="Cavalese cable car disaster (1998)">Cavalese cable car disaster</a>: a United States military pilot causes the deaths of 20 people near <a href="/wiki/Trento" title="Trento">Trento</a>, Italy, when his low-flying plane severs the cable of a cable-car.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_4" title="February 4">February 4</a> – The 5.9 <a href="/wiki/Moment_magnitude_scale" title="Moment magnitude scale">Mw</a> <a href="/wiki/February_1998_Afghanistan_earthquake" title="February 1998 Afghanistan earthquake">Afghanistan earthquake</a> shakes the <a href="/wiki/Takhar_Province" title="Takhar Province">Takhar Province</a> with a maximum <a href="/wiki/Mercalli_intensity_scale" title="Mercalli intensity scale">Mercalli intensity</a> of VII (<i>Very strong</i>). With 2,323 killed, and 818 injured, damage is considered extreme.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_7" title="February 7">February 7</a>–<a href="/wiki/February_22" title="February 22">22</a> – The <a href="/wiki/1998_Winter_Olympics" title="1998 Winter Olympics">1998 Winter Olympics</a> are held in <a href="/wiki/Nagano,_Nagano" title="Nagano, Nagano">Nagano</a>, <a href="/wiki/Japan" title="Japan">Japan</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_16" title="February 16">February 16</a> – <a href="/wiki/China_Airlines_Flight_676" title="China Airlines Flight 676">China Airlines Flight 676</a> crashes into a residential area near <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chiang_Kai-shek_International_Airport" title="Chiang Kai-shek International Airport">Chiang Kai-shek International Airport</a>, killing 202 people (all 196 on board and 6 on the ground).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_20" title="February 20">February 20</a> – <a href="/wiki/Iraq_disarmament_crisis" title="Iraq disarmament crisis">Iraq disarmament crisis</a>: Iraqi President <a href="/wiki/Saddam_Hussein" title="Saddam Hussein">Saddam Hussein</a> negotiates a deal with U.N. Secretary General <a href="/wiki/Kofi_Annan" title="Kofi Annan">Kofi Annan</a>, allowing weapons inspectors to return to <a href="/wiki/Baghdad" title="Baghdad">Baghdad</a>, preventing military action by the United States and Britain.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/February_28" title="February 28">February 28</a> – A <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Likoshane_massacre" title="Likoshane massacre">massacre</a> in Likoshane, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/FR_Yugoslavia" title="FR Yugoslavia">FR Yugoslavia</a> starts the <a href="/wiki/Kosovo_War" title="Kosovo War">Kosovo War</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="March">March</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: March">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_1" title="March 1">March 1</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Titanic_(1997_film)" title="Titanic (1997 film)">Titanic</a></i> becomes the first film to gross US$1 billion.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_2" title="March 2">March 2</a>
<ul>
<li>Data sent from the <a href="/wiki/Galileo_(spacecraft)" title="Galileo (spacecraft)">Galileo probe</a> indicates that Jupiter's moon <a href="/wiki/Europa_(moon)" title="Europa (moon)">Europa</a> has a liquid ocean under a thick crust of ice.</li>
<li>In Austria, <a href="/wiki/Natascha_Kampusch" title="Natascha Kampusch">Natascha Kampusch</a> is abducted by <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Wolfgang_P%C5%99iklopil" title="Wolfgang Přiklopil">Wolfgang Přiklopil</a> (she will remain in his captivity until August 2006).</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_5" title="March 5">March 5</a> – <a href="/wiki/NASA" title="NASA">NASA</a> announces that the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Clementine_mission" title="Clementine mission">Clementine</a> probe orbiting the Moon has found enough water in polar craters to support a human colony and rocket fueling station.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_11" title="March 11">March 11</a> – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Danish_parliamentary_election,_1998" title="Danish parliamentary election, 1998">Danish parliamentary election, 1998</a>: Prime Minister <a href="/wiki/Poul_Nyrup_Rasmussen" title="Poul Nyrup Rasmussen">Poul Nyrup Rasmussen</a> is re-elected.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_13" title="March 13">March 13</a> – The <a href="/wiki/High-Z_Supernova_Search_Team" title="High-Z Supernova Search Team">High-Z Supernova Search Team</a> becomes the first team to publish evidence that the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Accelerating_universe" title="Accelerating universe">universe is expanding at an accelerating rate</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_23" title="March 23">March 23</a> – The <a href="/wiki/70th_Academy_Awards" title="70th Academy Awards">70th Academy Awards</a> ceremony, hosted for the 6th time by <a href="/wiki/Billy_Crystal" title="Billy Crystal">Billy Crystal</a>, is held at the <a href="/wiki/Shrine_Auditorium" title="Shrine Auditorium">Shrine Auditorium</a> in Los Angeles, California. <i><a href="/wiki/Titanic_(1997_film)" title="Titanic (1997 film)">Titanic</a></i> wins 11 Oscars including <a href="/wiki/Academy_Award_for_Best_Picture" title="Academy Award for Best Picture">Best Picture</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_24" title="March 24">March 24</a> – First Computer-assisted <a href="/wiki/Bone_segment_navigation" title="Bone segment navigation">Bone Segment Navigation</a>, performed at the University of Regensburg, Germany.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_26" title="March 26">March 26</a> – <a href="/wiki/Oued_Bouaicha_massacre" title="Oued Bouaicha massacre">Oued Bouaicha massacre</a> in <a href="/wiki/Algeria" title="Algeria">Algeria</a>: 52 people are killed with axes and knives; 32 of the killed are babies under the age of 2.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_27" title="March 27">March 27</a> – <a href="/wiki/Sildenafil" title="Sildenafil">Sildenafil</a>, sold as Viagra and developed by <a href="/wiki/Pfizer" title="Pfizer">Pfizer</a>, is approved as the first oral treatment for erectile dysfunction in the USA by the <a href="/wiki/Food_and_Drug_Administration" title="Food and Drug Administration">Food and Drug Administration</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/March_31" title="March 31">March 31</a> – <a href="/wiki/Netscape" title="Netscape">Netscape</a> released <a href="/wiki/Mozilla" title="Mozilla">Mozilla</a> source code under an <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Open_source" title="Open source">open source</a> license. This is described in <a href="/wiki/The_Book_of_Mozilla#The_Book_of_Mozilla.2C_3:31" title="The Book of Mozilla">The Book of Mozilla, 3:31</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="April">April</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: April">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Akashi-kaikyo_bridge3.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="368" data-file-width="561" height="131" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Akashi-kaikyo_bridge3.jpg/200px-Akashi-kaikyo_bridge3.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Akashi-kaikyo_bridge3.jpg/300px-Akashi-kaikyo_bridge3.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/f5/Akashi-kaikyo_bridge3.jpg/400px-Akashi-kaikyo_bridge3.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Akashi-kaikyo_bridge3.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Akashi-Kaikyo Bridge</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_5" title="April 5">April 5</a> – In Japan, the <a href="/wiki/Akashi_Kaiky%C5%8D_Bridge" title="Akashi Kaikyō Bridge">Akashi Kaikyō Bridge</a> linking <a href="/wiki/Shikoku" title="Shikoku">Shikoku</a> with <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Honsh%C5%AB" title="Honshū">Honshū</a> and costing about US$3.8 billion, opens to traffic, becoming the largest <a href="/wiki/Suspension_bridge" title="Suspension bridge">suspension bridge</a> in the world.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_6" title="April 6">April 6</a> – <a href="/wiki/Pakistan" title="Pakistan">Pakistan</a> tests medium-range missiles capable of hitting India.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_10" title="April 10">April 10</a> – <a href="/wiki/Good_Friday_Agreement" title="Good Friday Agreement">Good Friday Agreement</a>: 1 hour after the end of the talks deadline, the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Belfast_Agreement" title="Belfast Agreement">Belfast Agreement</a> is signed between the Irish and British governments and most <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a> political parties, with the notable exception of the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Unionist_Party" title="Democratic Unionist Party">Democratic Unionist Party</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_20" title="April 20">April 20</a> – The alleged date the German <a href="/wiki/Red_Army_Faction" title="Red Army Faction">Red Army Faction</a> (created <a href="/wiki/1970" title="1970">1970</a>) is dissolved.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_22" title="April 22">April 22</a> – <a href="/wiki/Disney%27s_Animal_Kingdom" title="Disney's Animal Kingdom">Disney's Animal Kingdom</a> opens at <a href="/wiki/Walt_Disney_World" title="Walt Disney World">Walt Disney World</a> in <a href="/wiki/Orlando,_Florida" title="Orlando, Florida">Orlando, Florida</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/April_23" title="April 23">April 23</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Military_of_Serbia_and_Montenegro" title="Military of Serbia and Montenegro">Yugoslav Army</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/April_23,_1998_Albanian%E2%80%93Yugoslav_border_clashes" title="April 23, 1998 Albanian–Yugoslav border clashes">ambushes</a> a group of <a href="/wiki/Kosovo_Liberation_Army" title="Kosovo Liberation Army">Kosovo Liberation Army</a> fighters attempting to smuggle weapons from Albania into Kosovo, killing 19.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="May">May</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: May">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_8" title="May 8">May 8</a> – <a href="/wiki/CBS" title="CBS">CBS</a> telecasts <i><a href="/wiki/The_Wizard_of_Oz_(1939_film)" title="The Wizard of Oz (1939 film)">The Wizard of Oz</a></i> for the last time. Beginning in 1999, <i>The Wizard of Oz</i> will be shown on cable, and in 2002, 2003, 2004, and 2005 it will be telecast by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/WB_Television_Network" title="WB Television Network">WB Television Network</a> in addition to its cable showings.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_11" title="May 11">May 11</a>
<ul>
<li>India conducts 3 underground nuclear tests in <a href="/wiki/Pokhran" title="Pokhran">Pokhran</a>, including 1 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thermonuclear" title="Thermonuclear">thermonuclear</a> device.</li>
<li>The first <a href="/wiki/Euro" title="Euro">euro</a> coins are minted in <a href="/wiki/Pessac" title="Pessac">Pessac</a>, France. Because the final specifications for the coins were not finished in 1998, they will have to be melted and minted again in 1999.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_13" title="May 13">May 13</a>–<a href="/wiki/May_14" title="May 14">14</a> – <a href="/wiki/May_1998_riots_of_Indonesia" title="May 1998 riots of Indonesia">Riots directed against Chinese Indonesians</a> break out in Indonesia. Indonesian natives destroy and burn Chinese Indonesian-owned properties, however, most of the 1,000 people who died in the riots were the Javanese Indonesian looters who targeted the Chinese shops, not the Chinese themselves, since the looters were burnt to death in a massive fire.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4"><a href="#cite_note-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_19" title="May 19">May 19</a>
<ul>
<li>The <a href="/wiki/Galaxy_IV" title="Galaxy IV">Galaxy IV</a> communications satellite fails, leaving 80–90% of the world's pagers without service.</li>
<li>The wreck of the aircraft carrier <a href="/wiki/USS_Yorktown_(CV-5)" title="USS Yorktown (CV-5)">USS Yorktown</a>, sunk during the <a href="/wiki/Battle_of_Midway" title="Battle of Midway">Battle of Midway</a> in <a href="/wiki/1942" title="1942">1942</a>, is found near <a href="/wiki/Midway_Atoll" title="Midway Atoll">Midway Atoll</a> by a team led by former US Navy officer <a href="/wiki/Robert_Ballard" title="Robert Ballard">Robert D. Ballard</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_21" title="May 21">May 21</a> – <a href="/wiki/Suharto" title="Suharto">Suharto</a> (elected <a href="/wiki/1967" title="1967">1967</a>) resigns, after 32 years as <a href="/wiki/President_of_Indonesia" title="President of Indonesia">President of Indonesia</a> and his 7th consecutive re-election by the Indonesian Parliament (MPR). Suharto's hand-picked Vice President, <a href="/wiki/B._J._Habibie" title="B. J. Habibie">B. J. Habibie</a>, becomes Indonesia's third president.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_26" title="May 26">May 26</a> – <a href="/wiki/Bear_Grylls" title="Bear Grylls">Bear Grylls</a>, 23, becomes the youngest British climber to scale <a href="/wiki/Mount_Everest" title="Mount Everest">Mount Everest</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_28" title="May 28">May 28</a> – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nuclear_testing" title="Nuclear testing">Nuclear testing</a>: In response to a series of Indian nuclear tests, Pakistan explodes 5 nuclear devices of its own in the Chaghai hills of Baluchistan, codenamed <i><a href="/wiki/Chagai-I" title="Chagai-I">Chagai-I</a></i>, prompting the United States, Japan and other nations to impose <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Economic_sanction" title="Economic sanction">economic sanctions</a>. Pakistan celebrates <a href="/wiki/Youm-e-Takbir" title="Youm-e-Takbir">Youm-e-Takbir</a> annually.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/May_30" title="May 30">May 30</a>
<ul>
<li>A 6.6 magnitude earthquake hits northern <a href="/wiki/Afghanistan" title="Afghanistan">Afghanistan</a>, killing up to 5,000.</li>
<li>A second nuclear test, codenamed <i><a href="/wiki/Chagai-II" title="Chagai-II">Chagai-II</a></i>, is conducted and supervised by the <a href="/wiki/Pakistan_Atomic_Energy_Commission" title="Pakistan Atomic Energy Commission">Pakistan Atomic Energy Commission</a> (PAEC).</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="June">June</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: June">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Joseph_Estrada_1998.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1515" data-file-width="1044" height="290" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Joseph_Estrada_1998.jpg/200px-Joseph_Estrada_1998.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Joseph_Estrada_1998.jpg/300px-Joseph_Estrada_1998.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Joseph_Estrada_1998.jpg/400px-Joseph_Estrada_1998.jpg 2x" width="200"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Joseph_Estrada_1998.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
President <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Estrada" title="Joseph Estrada">Joseph Estrada</a></div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_2" title="June 2">June 2</a> – The <a href="/wiki/CIH_(computer_virus)" title="CIH (computer virus)">CIH computer virus</a> is discovered in <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_3" title="June 3">June 3</a> – <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Eschede_train_disaster" title="Eschede train disaster">Eschede train disaster</a>: An <a href="/wiki/Intercity-Express" title="Intercity-Express">Intercity-Express</a> <a href="/wiki/High-speed_rail" title="High-speed rail">high-speed train</a> derails between <a href="/wiki/Hanover" title="Hanover">Hanover</a> and <a href="/wiki/Hamburg" title="Hamburg">Hamburg</a>, Germany, causing 101 deaths.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_7" title="June 7">June 7</a>
<ul>
<li>Former Brigadier-General <a href="/wiki/Ansumane_Man%C3%A9" title="Ansumane Mané">Ansumane Mané</a> seizes control over military barracks in <a href="/wiki/Bissau" title="Bissau">Bissau</a>, marking the beginning of the <a href="/wiki/Guinea-Bissau_Civil_War" title="Guinea-Bissau Civil War">Guinea-Bissau Civil War</a> (1998–99).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Peter_Arnett" title="Peter Arnett">Peter Arnett</a> publishes a false report of <a href="/wiki/Operation_Tailwind" title="Operation Tailwind">Operation Tailwind</a> (initiated <a href="/wiki/1970" title="1970">1970</a>), claiming that <a href="/wiki/Sarin" title="Sarin">sarin</a> nerve agents were used to eliminate a group of deserting U.S. soldiers.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Murder_of_James_Byrd,_Jr." title="Murder of James Byrd, Jr.">James Byrd, Jr.</a> is beaten and dragged to death by 3 white men in <a href="/wiki/Jasper,_Texas" title="Jasper, Texas">Jasper, Texas</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_9" title="June 9">June 9</a>–<a href="/wiki/July_12" title="July 12">12</a> – The <a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1998 FIFA World Cup">1998 FIFA World Cup</a> begins in France.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_12" title="June 12">June 12</a> – The Centennial Celebration of Independence of the <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippines</a> from Spain is observed.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_25" title="June 25">June 25</a> – <a href="/wiki/Microsoft" title="Microsoft">Microsoft</a> releases <a href="/wiki/Windows_98" title="Windows 98">Windows 98</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_27" title="June 27">June 27</a> – <a href="/wiki/Kuala_Lumpur_International_Airport" title="Kuala Lumpur International Airport">Kuala Lumpur International Airport</a> officially opened, which also became the new international gateway into Malaysia.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/June_30" title="June 30">June 30</a> – <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">Philippine</a> Vice President <a href="/wiki/Joseph_Estrada" title="Joseph Estrada">Joseph Estrada</a> is sworn in as the 13th President of the Philippines.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="July">July</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: July">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_2" title="July 2">July 2</a> – <a href="/wiki/J._K._Rowling" title="J. K. Rowling">J. K. Rowling</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Harry_Potter_and_the_Chamber_of_Secrets" title="Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets">Harry Potter and the Chamber of Secrets</a> is published.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_5" title="July 5">July 5</a> – Japan launches a probe to <a href="/wiki/Mars" title="Mars">Mars</a>, joining the United States and Russia as an <a href="/wiki/Outer_space" title="Outer space">outer space</a>-exploring nation.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_6" title="July 6">July 6</a> – The new <a href="/wiki/Hong_Kong_International_Airport" title="Hong Kong International Airport">Hong Kong International Airport</a> at <a href="/wiki/Chek_Lap_Kok" title="Chek Lap Kok">Chek Lap Kok</a> opens, while the old <a href="/wiki/Kai_Tak_Airport" title="Kai Tak Airport">Kai Tak Airport</a> closes.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_12" title="July 12">July 12</a> – <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> beats <a href="/wiki/Brazil_national_football_team" title="Brazil national football team">Brazil</a> 3–0 in the <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">football</a> <a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1998 FIFA World Cup">World Cup</a> <a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="1998 FIFA World Cup Final">final</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_17" title="July 17">July 17</a>
<ul>
<li>At a conference in <a href="/wiki/Rome" title="Rome">Rome</a>, 120 countries vote to create a permanent <a href="/wiki/International_Criminal_Court" title="International Criminal Court">International Criminal Court</a> to prosecute individuals for genocide, <a href="/wiki/Crimes_against_humanity" title="Crimes against humanity">crimes against humanity</a>, <a href="/wiki/War_crime" title="War crime">war crimes</a>, and the <a href="/wiki/Crime_of_aggression" title="Crime of aggression">crime of aggression</a>.</li>
<li>In <a href="/wiki/Saint_Petersburg" title="Saint Petersburg">Saint Petersburg</a>, <a href="/wiki/Nicholas_II_of_Russia" title="Nicholas II of Russia">Nicholas II of Russia</a> and his family are buried in St. Catherine Chapel, 80 years after he and his family were killed by the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lenin" title="Lenin">Lenin</a>-led <a href="/wiki/Bolsheviks" title="Bolsheviks">Bolsheviks</a> in <a href="/wiki/1918" title="1918">1918</a>.</li>
<li>The 7.0 <a href="/wiki/Moment_magnitude_scale" title="Moment magnitude scale">Mw</a> <a href="/wiki/1998_Papua_New_Guinea_earthquake" title="1998 Papua New Guinea earthquake">Papua New Guinea earthquake</a> shakes the region near <a href="/wiki/Aitape" title="Aitape">Aitape</a> with a maximum <a href="/wiki/Mercalli_intensity_scale" title="Mercalli intensity scale">Mercalli intensity</a> of VIII (<i>Severe</i>). This <a href="/wiki/Submarine_earthquake" title="Submarine earthquake">submarine earthquake</a> triggered a landslide that caused a destructive tsunami, leaving 2,183–2,700 dead and thousands injured.</li>
<li>Biologists report in the journal <i><a href="/wiki/Science_(journal)" title="Science (journal)">Science</a></i> how they sequenced the <a href="/wiki/Genome" title="Genome">genome</a> of the bacterium that causes syphilis, <i><a href="/wiki/Treponema_pallidum" title="Treponema pallidum">Treponema pallidum</a></i>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/July_24" title="July 24">July 24</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Saving_Private_Ryan" title="Saving Private Ryan">Saving Private Ryan</a></i> premieres in theaters.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="August">August</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: August">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:122px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Kenya_bombing_1.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="286" data-file-width="187" height="184" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Kenya_bombing_1.jpg/120px-Kenya_bombing_1.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Kenya_bombing_1.jpg/180px-Kenya_bombing_1.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/0/0b/Kenya_bombing_1.jpg 2x" width="120"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Kenya_bombing_1.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
<a href="/wiki/August_7" title="August 7">Aug.7</a>: Nairobi Embassy bombing.</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_4" title="August 4">August 4</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Second_Congo_War" title="Second Congo War">Second Congo War</a> begins; 3,900,000 people are killed before it ends in <a href="/wiki/2003" title="2003">2003</a>, making it the bloodiest war, to date, since World War II.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_7" title="August 7">August 7</a>
<ul>
<li>Yangtze River Floods: In China the <a href="/wiki/Yangtze" title="Yangtze">Yangtze</a> river breaks through the main bank; before this, from August 1–5, peripheral levees collapsed consecutively in Jiayu County Baizhou Bay. The death toll exceeds 12,000, with many thousands more injured.</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/1998_U.S._embassy_bombings" title="1998 U.S. embassy bombings">1998 U.S. embassy bombings</a>: The bombings of the United States embassies in <a href="/wiki/Dar_es_Salaam" title="Dar es Salaam">Dar es Salaam</a>, Tanzania, and <a href="/wiki/Nairobi" title="Nairobi">Nairobi</a>, Kenya, kill 224 people and injure over 4,500; they are linked to terrorist <a href="/wiki/Osama_bin_Laden" title="Osama bin Laden">Osama bin Laden</a>, an exile of <a href="/wiki/Saudi_Arabia" title="Saudi Arabia">Saudi Arabia</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_15" title="August 15">August 15</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Omagh_bombing" title="Omagh bombing">Omagh bombing</a> is carried out in <a href="/wiki/Northern_Ireland" title="Northern Ireland">Northern Ireland</a> by the Real IRA.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_24" title="August 24">August 24</a> – The first <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/RFID" title="RFID">RFID</a> human implantation is tested in the United Kingdom.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/August_26" title="August 26">August 26</a> – Computer virus <a href="/wiki/CIH_(computer_virus)" title="CIH (computer virus)">CIH</a> activates and attacks <a href="/wiki/Windows_9x" title="Windows 9x">Windows 9x</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="September">September</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: September">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright">
<div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Hudson03.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1276" data-file-width="2100" height="134" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Hudson03.jpg/220px-Hudson03.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Hudson03.jpg/330px-Hudson03.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c8/Hudson03.jpg/440px-Hudson03.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a>
<div class="thumbcaption">
<div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Hudson03.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>
Canadian Coast Guard Vessel Henry Hudson searches for <a href="/wiki/Swissair_Flight_111" title="Swissair Flight 111">Swissair Flight 111</a> debris</div>
</div>
</div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_2" title="September 2">September 2</a>
<ul>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/McDonnell_Douglas_MD-11" title="McDonnell Douglas MD-11">McDonnell Douglas MD-11</a> airliner (<a href="/wiki/Swissair_Flight_111" title="Swissair Flight 111">Swissair Flight 111</a>) crashes near <a href="/wiki/Peggys_Cove,_Nova_Scotia" title="Peggys Cove, Nova Scotia">Peggys Cove, Nova Scotia</a>, after taking off from New York City en route to <a href="/wiki/Geneva" title="Geneva">Geneva</a>; all 229 people on board are killed.</li>
<li>A <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">United Nations</a> court finds <a href="/wiki/Jean-Paul_Akayesu" title="Jean-Paul Akayesu">Jean-Paul Akayesu</a>, the former mayor of a small town in <a href="/wiki/Rwanda" title="Rwanda">Rwanda</a>, guilty of 9 counts of genocide, marking the first time that the <a href="/wiki/1948" title="1948">1948</a> law banning genocide is enforced.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_4" title="September 4">September 4</a>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Google" title="Google">Google</a>, Inc. is founded in <a href="/wiki/Menlo_Park,_California" title="Menlo Park, California">Menlo Park, California</a>, by <a href="/wiki/Stanford_University" title="Stanford University">Stanford University</a> PhD candidates <a href="/wiki/Larry_Page" title="Larry Page">Larry Page</a> and <a href="/wiki/Sergey_Brin" title="Sergey Brin">Sergey Brin</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></li>
<li>The last former <a href="/wiki/Soviet_Union" title="Soviet Union">Soviet Union</a> radar station, <a href="/wiki/Skrunda-1" title="Skrunda-1">Skrunda-1</a>, is closed down in <a href="/wiki/Latvia" title="Latvia">Latvia</a>.</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_5" title="September 5">September 5</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_North_Korea" title="Politics of North Korea">Government</a> of <a href="/wiki/North_Korea" title="North Korea">North Korea</a> adopts a military dictatorship on its 50th anniversary.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_10" title="September 10">September 10</a> – At midnight, a <a href="/wiki/Russian_submarine_Vepr_(K-157)#1998_incident" title="Russian submarine Vepr (K-157)">shooting occurs</a> aboard an <a href="/wiki/Akula-class_submarine" title="Akula-class submarine"><i>Akula</i>-class</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nuclear-powered" title="Nuclear-powered">nuclear-powered</a> <a href="/wiki/Attack_submarine" title="Attack submarine">attack submarine</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Russian_Navy" title="Russian Navy">Russian Navy</a> docked in the northern Russian port-city of <a href="/wiki/Severomorsk" title="Severomorsk">Severomorsk</a>. The shooter, Alexander Kuzminykh, a 19-year-old seaman from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/St._Petersburg" title="St. Petersburg">St. Petersburg</a>, opened fire after murdering a soldier (who was supervising his detention on punishment charges in the personnel quarters of <a href="/wiki/Russian_submarine_Vepr_(K-157)" title="Russian submarine Vepr (K-157)">the submarine</a>) with a <a href="/wiki/Chisel" title="Chisel">chisel</a>, and taking his <a href="/wiki/AK-74#AKS-74U" title="AK-74">AK-74U</a> <a href="/wiki/Carbine" title="Carbine">carbine</a>. After killing five people and wounding one with the dead soldier's weapon, he proceeded to take 2 fellow soldiers <a href="/wiki/Hostage" title="Hostage">hostage</a>, and barricaded himself in the submarine's torpedo room, where he would later murder them. For 23 hours, doctors, relatives, and a priest attempt to persuade him to surrender, but to no avail. After threatening numerous times to set the torpedo room on fire (an event the authorities feared would cause a quote "second <a href="/wiki/Chernobyl" title="Chernobyl">Chernobyl</a>"), the crisis came to an end on the morning of 12 September, when a special <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Anti-terrorist" title="Anti-terrorist">anti-terrorist</a> commando unit of the Russian <a href="/wiki/Federal_Security_Service" title="Federal Security Service">Federal Security Service</a> (FSB) launched a raid on the torpedo room during which, Kuzminkykh allegedly committed <a href="/wiki/Suicide" title="Suicide">suicide</a>, contrary to prior reports that he'd been killed by the unit.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_12" title="September 12">September 12</a> - The <a href="/wiki/Cuban_Five" title="Cuban Five">Cuban Five</a> intelligence agents are arrested in <a href="/wiki/Miami" title="Miami">Miami</a>, and convicted of <a href="/wiki/Espionage" title="Espionage">espionage</a>. The agents claim they were not spying against the <a href="/wiki/Federal_government_of_the_United_States" title="Federal government of the United States">United States Government</a> but against the <a href="/wiki/Cuban_exile" title="Cuban exile">Cuban exile</a> community in Miami.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/September_24" title="September 24">September 24</a> – <a href="/wiki/President_of_Iran" title="President of Iran">Iranian President</a> <a href="/wiki/Mohammad_Khatami" title="Mohammad Khatami">Mohammad Khatami</a> retracts a fatwa against <i><a href="/wiki/The_Satanic_Verses" title="The Satanic Verses">Satanic Verses</a></i> author <a href="/wiki/Salman_Rushdie" title="Salman Rushdie">Salman Rushdie</a> that was in force since <a href="/wiki/1989" title="1989">1989</a> stating that the Iranian government will "neither support nor hinder assassination operations on Rushdie".</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="October">October</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: October">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_6" title="October 6">October 6</a> – <a href="/wiki/Matthew_Shepard" title="Matthew Shepard">Matthew Shepard</a> is beaten and left to die in a cornfield in <a href="/wiki/Laramie,_Wyoming" title="Laramie, Wyoming">Laramie, Wyoming</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_14" title="October 14">October 14</a> – <a href="/wiki/Eric_Rudolph" title="Eric Rudolph">Eric Rudolph</a> is charged with 4 bombings (including the <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/1996_Olympic_bombing" title="1996 Olympic bombing">1996 Olympic bombing</a>) in <a href="/wiki/Atlanta" title="Atlanta">Atlanta</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_16" title="October 16">October 16</a> – British police place General <a href="/wiki/Augusto_Pinochet" title="Augusto Pinochet">Augusto Pinochet</a>, the former <a href="/wiki/Chile" title="Chile">Chilean</a> dictator from <a href="/wiki/1973" title="1973">1973</a>-<a href="/wiki/1990" title="1990">1990</a>, under house arrest during his medical treatment in the UK.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_17" title="October 17">October 17</a> – A <a href="/wiki/1998_Jesse_pipeline_explosion" title="1998 Jesse pipeline explosion">pipeline explosion</a> in Jesse, <a href="/wiki/Nigeria" title="Nigeria">Nigeria</a> results in 1,082 deaths.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/October_29" title="October 29">October 29</a> – <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Mitch" title="Hurricane Mitch">Hurricane Mitch</a> makes landfall in Central America, killing an estimated 18,000 people.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="November">November</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: November">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_16" title="November 16">November 16</a> – <a href="/wiki/Sesame_Workshop" title="Sesame Workshop">Sesame Workshop</a> (then known as <b>Children's Television Workshop</b>) launches <a href="/wiki/Elmo%27s_World" title="Elmo's World">Elmo's World</a>, the most famous <a href="/wiki/Sesame_Street" title="Sesame Street">Sesame Street</a> segment, lasting from the late 90' to Sesame Street's 40th anniversary (69-09) and the 10th anniversary of the segment itself (99-09).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_17" title="November 17">November 17</a> – <i><a href="/wiki/Voyager_1" title="Voyager 1">Voyager 1</a></i> overtakes <i><a href="/wiki/Pioneer_10" title="Pioneer 10">Pioneer 10</a></i> as the most distant man-made object from the <a href="/wiki/Solar_System" title="Solar System">Solar System</a>, at a distance of 69.419 AU (1.03849<span style="margin:0 .15em 0 .25em">×</span>10<sup>10</sup> km).</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_20" title="November 20">November 20</a> – A Russian <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Proton_rocket" title="Proton rocket">Proton rocket</a> is launched from the <a href="/wiki/Baikonur_Cosmodrome" title="Baikonur Cosmodrome">Baikonur Cosmodrome</a> in <a href="/wiki/Kazakhstan" title="Kazakhstan">Kazakhstan</a>, carrying the first segment of the <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">International Space Station</a>, the 21-ton <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Zarya_Module" title="Zarya Module">Zarya Module</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_21" title="November 21">November 21</a> – <a href="/wiki/Nintendo" title="Nintendo">Nintendo</a> releases <a href="/wiki/The_Legend_of_Zelda:_Ocarina_of_Time" title="The Legend of Zelda: Ocarina of Time">The Legend of Zelda: Ocarina of Time</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/November_24" title="November 24">November 24</a> – A declassified report by Swiss <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/IOC" title="IOC">IOC</a> official <a href="/wiki/Marc_Hodler" title="Marc Hodler">Marc Hodler</a> reveals that bribes had been used to bring the <a href="/wiki/2002_Winter_Olympics" title="2002 Winter Olympics">2002 Winter Olympics</a> to <a href="/wiki/Salt_Lake_City" title="Salt Lake City">Salt Lake City</a> during bidding process in <a href="/wiki/1995" title="1995">1995</a>. The International Olympic Committee, the <a href="/wiki/Salt_Lake_Organizing_Committee_for_the_Olympic_and_Paralympic_Winter_Games_of_2002" title="Salt Lake Organizing Committee for the Olympic and Paralympic Winter Games of 2002">Salt Lake Organizing Committee</a>, the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Olympic_Committee" title="United States Olympic Committee">United States Olympic Committee</a> and the <a href="/wiki/United_States_Department_of_Justice" title="United States Department of Justice">United States Department of Justice</a> immediately launch an investigation into the <a href="/wiki/2002_Winter_Olympic_bid_scandal" title="2002 Winter Olympic bid scandal">scandal</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="December">December</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: December">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_4" title="December 4">December 4</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Space_Shuttle_Endeavour" title="Space Shuttle Endeavour">Space Shuttle Endeavour</a> launches the first American component to the <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">International Space Station</a>, the 25,600 lb <a href="/wiki/Unity_(ISS_module)" title="Unity (ISS module)">Unity</a> module on <a href="/wiki/STS-88" title="STS-88">STS-88</a>. It docks with Zarya two days later.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_6" title="December 6">December 6</a> – <a href="/wiki/Hugo_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Hugo Chávez">Hugo Chávez</a>, politician and former member of the Venezuelan military, is <a href="/wiki/Venezuelan_presidential_election,_1998" title="Venezuelan presidential election, 1998">elected</a> President of <a href="/wiki/Venezuela" title="Venezuela">Venezuela</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_14" title="December 14">December 14</a> – The <a href="/wiki/Military_of_Serbia_and_Montenegro" title="Military of Serbia and Montenegro">Yugoslav Army</a> <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/December_14,_1998_Albanian%E2%80%93Yugoslav_border_clashes" title="December 14, 1998 Albanian–Yugoslav border clashes">ambushes</a> a column of 140 <a href="/wiki/Kosovo_Liberation_Army" title="Kosovo Liberation Army">Kosovo Liberation Army</a> militants attempting to smuggle arms from Albania into Kosovo, killing 36.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_16" title="December 16">December 16</a>–<a href="/wiki/December_19" title="December 19">19</a> – <a href="/wiki/Iraq_disarmament_crisis" title="Iraq disarmament crisis">Iraq disarmament crisis</a>: U.S. President <a href="/wiki/Bill_Clinton" title="Bill Clinton">Bill Clinton</a> orders airstrikes on <a href="/wiki/Iraq" title="Iraq">Iraq</a>. UNSCOM withdraws all weapons inspectors from Iraq.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_19" title="December 19">December 19</a> – The <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/U.S._House_of_Representatives" title="U.S. House of Representatives">U.S. House of Representatives</a> forwards <a href="/wiki/Impeachment_of_Bill_Clinton" title="Impeachment of Bill Clinton">articles of impeachment against President Clinton</a> to the Senate, making him the second president to be impeached in the nation.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_29" title="December 29">December 29</a> – <a href="/wiki/Khmer_Rouge" title="Khmer Rouge">Khmer Rouge</a> leaders apologize for the post-<a href="/wiki/Vietnam_War" title="Vietnam War">Vietnam War</a> <a href="/wiki/Genocide" title="Genocide">genocide</a> in <a href="/wiki/Cambodia" title="Cambodia">Cambodia</a> that claimed over 1 million in the <a href="/wiki/1970s" title="1970s">1970s</a>.</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/December_31" title="December 31">December 31</a> – The first <a href="/wiki/Leap_second" title="Leap second">leap second</a> since June 30, 1997, occurs. In the <a href="/wiki/Eurozone" title="Eurozone">eurozone</a>, the currency rates of this day are fixed permanently.</li>
</ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Date_unknown">Date unknown</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Date unknown">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul>
<li>Ibrahim Hanna, the last native speaker of <a href="/wiki/Mlahs%C3%B4_language" title="Mlahsô language">Mlahsô</a>, dies in <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Qamishli" title="Qamishli">Qamishli</a>, <a href="/wiki/Syria" title="Syria">Syria</a>, making the language effectively extinct. Also, the last native speaker of related <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Bijil_Neo-Aramaic" title="Bijil Neo-Aramaic">Bijil Neo-Aramaic</a>, Mrs. Rahel Avraham, dies in <a href="/wiki/Jerusalem" title="Jerusalem">Jerusalem</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></li>
<li>Italian <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Road_racing_cyclist" title="Road racing cyclist">road racing cyclist</a> <a href="/wiki/Marco_Pantani" title="Marco Pantani">Marco Pantani</a> wins both the <a href="/wiki/Tour_de_France" title="Tour de France">Tour de France</a> and <a href="/wiki/Giro_d%27Italia" title="Giro d'Italia">Giro d'Italia</a> this year.</li>
</ul>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Nobel_Prizes">Nobel Prizes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Nobel Prizes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="floatright"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Nobel_medal.png"><img alt="Nobel medal.png" data-file-height="1013" data-file-width="1013" height="100" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6a/Nobel_medal.png/100px-Nobel_medal.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6a/Nobel_medal.png/150px-Nobel_medal.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/en/thumb/6/6a/Nobel_medal.png/200px-Nobel_medal.png 2x" width="100"/></a></div>
<ul>
<li><a href="/wiki/Nobel_Prize_in_Physics" title="Nobel Prize in Physics">Physics</a> – <a href="/wiki/Robert_B._Laughlin" title="Robert B. Laughlin">Robert B. Laughlin</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Horst_L._St%C3%B6rmer" title="Horst L. Störmer">Horst L. Störmer</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Daniel_Chee_Tsui" title="Daniel Chee Tsui">Daniel Chee Tsui</a></li>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Fields_Medal">Fields Medal</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=42" title="Edit section: Fields Medal">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Richard_Ewen_Borcherds" title="Richard Ewen Borcherds">Richard Ewen Borcherds</a>, <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/William_Timothy_Gowers" title="William Timothy Gowers">William Timothy Gowers</a>, <a href="/wiki/Maxim_Kontsevich" title="Maxim Kontsevich">Maxim Kontsevich</a>, <a href="/wiki/Curtis_T._McMullen" title="Curtis T. McMullen">Curtis T. McMullen</a></li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="In_fiction">In fiction</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=1998&amp;action=edit&amp;section=43" title="Edit section: In fiction">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul>
<li>The Japanese horror novel <i><a href="/wiki/Another_(novel)" title="Another (novel)">Another</a></i> is set in the fictional town of Yomiyama, Japan during 1998.</li>
<li>The novel <i><a href="/wiki/Adrian_Mole:_The_Cappuccino_Years" title="Adrian Mole: The Cappuccino Years">Adrian Mole: The Cappuccino Years</a></i> takes place from April 30, 1997, to May 2, 1998.</li>
<li>The video games <i><a href="/wiki/Resident_Evil_Zero" title="Resident Evil Zero">Resident Evil Zero</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Resident_Evil_(1996_video_game)" title="Resident Evil (1996 video game)">Resident Evil</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Resident_Evil_2" title="Resident Evil 2">Resident Evil 2</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Resident_Evil_3:_Nemesis" title="Resident Evil 3: Nemesis">Resident Evil 3: Nemesis</a></i>, <i><a href="/wiki/Resident_Evil:_Operation_Raccoon_City" title="Resident Evil: Operation Raccoon City">Resident Evil: Operation Raccoon City</a></i>, and <i><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Resident_Evil_Code:_Veronica" title="Resident Evil Code: Veronica">Resident Evil Code: Veronica</a></i> all take place in 1998, July for the first two, September for the next three, and December CV.</li>
<li>In the Resident Evil franchise, Raccoon City is destroyed on October 1, 1998.</li>
<li>The video game <a href="/wiki/Grand_Theft_Auto:_Liberty_City_Stories" title="Grand Theft Auto: Liberty City Stories">Grand Theft Auto: Liberty City Stories</a> is set in 1998</li>
<li>The TV series <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ben_10_(TV_series)" title="Ben 10 (TV series)">Ben 10</a> is set in 1998.</li>
</ul>
